Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

Display all categories

This method is used to display all categories.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/categories" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/categories"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 58
vary: Origin

GET api/states

This method is used to create a new state.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/states" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"keiezpgtlzbfoxjjsrgqwprwie\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/states"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "keiezpgtlzbfoxjjsrgqwprwie"
};

    method: "POST",
    headers,

}).then(response => response.json());

Store a newly created developer in storage.

This method is used to create a new developer.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/workers" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"kyrjhoblkecyejujceqokwsmvefbvyxyenyyxxfbiyaemeeyvesoayfsrkbdynyzyukaiezramjjtccwbvmdwhfqlzjvgqlivlrceobumfaurutlhuswszmavcau\",
    \"passport\": \"quo\",
    \"family\": \"sequi\",
    \"developer_photo\": \"aliquid\",
    \"born_date\": \"ut\",
    \"phone_number\": \"est\",
    \"work_type_id\": \"vel\",
    \"about\": \"et\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/workers"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "kyrjhoblkecyejujceqokwsmvefbvyxyenyyxxfbiyaemeeyvesoayfsrkbdynyzyukaiezramjjtccwbvmdwhfqlzjvgqlivlrceobumfaurutlhuswszmavcau",
    "passport": "quo",
    "family": "sequi",
    "developer_photo": "aliquid",
    "born_date": "ut",
    "phone_number": "est",
    "work_type_id": "vel",
    "about": "et"
};

    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

GET api/directions

Store a newly created type in storage.

This method is used to create a new type.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/directions" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"ktrxonuaxuxqvdlnjeajxidvctkvfbpaoquymplpmqlswdshyryhgddqjolqwerlxpekjhikqooueqwsrrakekwfhbsafxsldgfbyonkchmjhpcpymkwhcgzoquumfckovdzcxezly\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/directions"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "ktrxonuaxuxqvdlnjeajxidvctkvfbpaoquymplpmqlswdshyryhgddqjolqwerlxpekjhikqooueqwsrrakekwfhbsafxsldgfbyonkchmjhpcpymkwhcgzoquumfckovdzcxezly"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
